Action.c(78):     **     text\n

Action.c(78):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isCheck(formObj, form, [index of first checkbox in group],\n
Action.c(78):     **         [number of checkboxes])\n

Action.c(78):     function validation(realName, formEltName, eltType, upToSnuff, format) {\n
Action.c(78):       this.realName = realName;\n
Action.c(78):       this.formEltName = formEltName;\n
Action.c(78):       this.eltType = eltType;\n
Action.c(78):       this.upToSnuff = upToSnuff;\n
Action.c(78):       this.format = format;\n
Action.c(78):     }\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(78):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n
Action.c(78):     ** for example:\n
Action.c(78):     ** var lastName = new validation('last name', 'lastName', 'text', 'isText(str)', null);\n
Action.c(78):     ** var phoneNum = new validation('phone number', 'phoneNum', 'text', 'isPhoneNum(str)', 'x
Action.c(78):     xx-xxx-xxxx');\n

Action.c(78):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(78):     ** The main function keeps track of which fields the user missed\n
Action.c(78):     ** or filled in incorrectly, and alerts the user so they can go\n
Action.c(78):     ** back and fix what's wrong.\n

Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(78):     ** change text for alerts here\n
Action.c(78):     ** unspecified field (text): "Please include [field name]."\n
Action.c(78):     ** unspecified field (other): "Please choose [field name]."\n

Action.c(78):     var beginRequestAlertForText = "Please include ";\n

Action.c(78):     var beginInvalidAlert = " is an invalid ";\n
Action.c(78):     var endInvalidAlert = "!";\n
Action.c(78):     var beginFormatAlert = "  Use this format: ";\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(78):     ** these functions validate the string or form object passed in,\n
Action.c(78):     ** and return true or false based on whether the test succeeds or fails\n
Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     ** validate existence of input\n
Action.c(78):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n
Action.c(78):     **   isSelect(formObj): verifies item from a select menu is chosen\n
Action.c(78):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Action.c(78):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Action.c(78):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n
Action.c(78):     **     for [begin], fill in the index number in the elements array\n
Action.c(78):     **         of the first checkbox (remember to start counting from zero)\n
Action.c(78):     **     for [num], fill in the number of checkboxes in the group\n
Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     ** validate text in text input or textarea matches pattern\n
Action.c(78):     **   isEmail(str): verifies email address (contains "@" and ".")\n
Action.c(78):     **   isState(str): verifies U.S. State Code\n
Action.c(78):     **   isZipCode(str): verifies zip code of form xxxxx or xxxxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(78):     **   isPhoneNum(str): verifies phone number of form xxx-xxx-xxxx\n
Action.c(78):     **   isDate(str): verifies date of form mm/dd/yyyy\n
Action.c(78):     ***************************************************************/\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     function isText(str) {\n
Action.c(78):       return (str != "");\n
Action.c(78):     }\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     function isSelect(formObj) {\n
Action.c(78):       return (formObj.selectedIndex != 0);\n
Action.c(78):     }\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     function isRadio(formObj) {\n
Action.c(78):       for (j=0; j<formObj.length; j++) {\n
Action.c(78):         if (formObj[j].checked) {\n
Action.c(78):           return true;\n
Action.c(78):         }\n
Action.c(78):       }\n
Action.c(78):       return false;\n

Action.c(78):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(78):     ** define and instantiate validation objects\n
Action.c(78):     ** the validation object accepts the following parameters:\n
Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     **   realName: name used in the alerts (same as label on the page)\n
Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     **   formEltName: this must be the name of the corresponding\n
Action.c(78):     **       HTML form element; make it the same as the object name\n
Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     **   eltType: element type (we have to create this since IE3\n
Action.c(78):     **       doesn't support the type property for for elements)\n
Action.c(78):     **     text\n
Action.c(78):     **     textarea\n
Action.c(78):     **     checkbox\n
Action.c(78):     **     radio\n
Action.c(78):     **     select\n
Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     **   uptoSnuff: function call that's evaluated during validation check\n
Action.c(78):     **     isText(str)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isSelect(formObj)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isRadio(formObj)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isCheck(formObj, form, [index of first checkbox in group],\n
Action.c(78):     **         [number of checkboxes])\n
Action.c(78):     **     isEmail(str)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isState(str)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isZipCode(str)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isPhoneNum(str)\n
Action.c(78):     **     isDate(str)\n
Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     **   format: text representation of required format;\n
Action.c(78):     **       pass 'null' if no required format;\n
Action.c(78):     **       used in alert as an aid to user\n
Action.c(78):     ***************************************************************/\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     // object definition\n
Action.c(78):     function validation(realName, formEltName, eltType, upToSnuff, format) {\n
Action.c(78):       this.realName = realName;\n
Action.c(78):       this.formEltName = formEltName;\n
Action.c(78):       this.eltType = eltType;\n
Action.c(78):       this.upToSnuff = upToSnuff;\n
Action.c(78):       this.format = format;\n
Action.c(78):     }\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(78):     ** create a new object for each form element you need to validate\n

Action.c(78):     ** var phoneNum = new validation('phone number', 'phoneNum', 'text', 'isPhoneNum(str)', 'x
Action.c(78):     xx-xxx-xxxx');\n

Action.c(78):     /***************************************************************\n
Action.c(78):     ** these functions validate the string or form object passed in,\n

Action.c(78):     **\n
Action.c(78):     ** validate existence of input\n
Action.c(78):     **   isText(str): verifies text input or textarea is not empty\n
Action.c(78):     **   isSelect(formObj): verifies item from a select menu is chosen\n
Action.c(78):     **   isRadio(formObj): verifies one of a group of radio buttons is chosen\n
Action.c(78):     **   isCheck(formObj, form, [begin], [num]): verifies at least one\n
Action.c(78):     **       of a group of checkboxes is checked\n

Action.c(78):     function validateForm(form) {\n
Action.c(78):       var formEltName = "";\n
Action.c(78):       var formObj = "";\n
Action.c(78):       var str = "";\n
Action.c(78):       var realName = "";\n

Action.c(78):       var hardReturn = "\\r\\n";\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):       for (i=0; i<elts.length; i++) {\n
Action.c(78):         formEltName = elts[i].formEltName;\n
Action.c(78):         formObj = eval("form." + formEltName);\n
Action.c(78):         realName = elts[i].realName;\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):         if (elts[i].eltType == "text") {\n
Action.c(78):           str = formObj.value;\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):           if (eval(elts[i].upToSnuff)) continue;\n
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):           if (str == "") {\n
Action.c(78):             if (allAtOnce) {\n
Action.c(78):               alertText += beginRequestAlertForText + realName + endRequestAlert + hardReturn;
Action.c(78):     \n
Action.c(78):               if (firstMissingElt == null) {firstMissingElt = formObj};\n
Action.c(78):             } else {\n
Action.c(78):               alertText = beginRequestAlertForText + realName + endRequestAlert + hardReturn;\n
Action.c(78):               alert(alertText);\n
Action.c(78):             }\n
Action.c(78):           } else {\n
Action.c(78):             if (allAtOnce) {\n
